\DoxyCodeLine{821 \textcolor{comment}{// polymorphic\_type\_hook<itype>::get(src, tinfo) determines whether the object pointed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{822 \textcolor{comment}{// to by `src` actually is an instance of some class derived from `itype`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{823 \textcolor{comment}{// If so, it sets `tinfo` to point to the std::type\_info representing that derived}}
\DoxyCodeLine{824 \textcolor{comment}{// type, and returns a pointer to the start of the most-\/derived object of that type}}
\DoxyCodeLine{825 \textcolor{comment}{// (in which `src` is a subobject; this will be the same address as `src` in most}}
\DoxyCodeLine{826 \textcolor{comment}{// single inheritance cases). If not, or if `src` is nullptr, it simply returns `src`}}
\DoxyCodeLine{827 \textcolor{comment}{// and leaves `tinfo` at its default value of nullptr.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{828 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{829 \textcolor{comment}{// The default polymorphic\_type\_hook just returns src. A specialization for polymorphic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{830 \textcolor{comment}{// types determines the runtime type of the passed object and adjusts the this-\/pointer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{831 \textcolor{comment}{// appropriately via dynamic\_cast<void*>. This is what enables a C++ Animal* to appear}}
\DoxyCodeLine{832 \textcolor{comment}{// to Python as a Dog (if Dog inherits from Animal, Animal is polymorphic, Dog is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{833 \textcolor{comment}{// registered with pybind11, and this Animal is in fact a Dog).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{834 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{835 \textcolor{comment}{// You may specialize polymorphic\_type\_hook yourself for types that want to appear}}
\DoxyCodeLine{836 \textcolor{comment}{// polymorphic to Python but do not use C++ RTTI. (This is a not uncommon pattern}}
\DoxyCodeLine{837 \textcolor{comment}{// in performance-\/sensitive applications, used most notably in LLVM.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{838 \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} itype, \textcolor{keyword}{typename} SFINAE = \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}>}
\DoxyCodeLine{839 \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{structpolymorphic__type__hook}{polymorphic\_type\_hook}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{840 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{841     \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} *\mbox{\hyperlink{structpolymorphic__type__hook_ab5a3e418474aeaf2a919ad6c0db53d15}{get}}(\textcolor{keyword}{const} itype *src, \textcolor{keyword}{const} std::type\_info*\&) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} src; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{842 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{843 \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} itype>}

\DoxyCodeLine{1354         \textcolor{comment}{// If we're in UTF-\/8 mode, we have two possible failures: one for a unicode character that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1355         \textcolor{comment}{// is too high, and one for multiple unicode characters (caught later), so we need to figure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1356         \textcolor{comment}{// out how long the first encoded character is in bytes to distinguish between these two}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1357         \textcolor{comment}{// errors.  We also allow want to allow unicode characters U+0080 through U+00FF, as those}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1358         \textcolor{comment}{// can fit into a single char value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1359         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (StringCaster::UTF\_N == 8 \&\& str\_len > 1 \&\& str\_len <= 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1360             \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} v0 = \textcolor{keyword}{static\_cast<}\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}\textcolor{keyword}{>}(\mbox{\hyperlink{classtype__caster__generic_a077b8d1e4af829443b2e41c3e5786f4d}{value}}[0]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1361             \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} char0\_bytes = !(v0 \& 0x80) ? 1 : \textcolor{comment}{// low bits only: 0-\/127}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1362                 (v0 \& 0xE0) == 0xC0 ? 2 : \textcolor{comment}{// 0b110xxxxx -\/ start of 2-\/byte sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1363                 (v0 \& 0xF0) == 0xE0 ? 3 : \textcolor{comment}{// 0b1110xxxx -\/ start of 3-\/byte sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1364                 4; \textcolor{comment}{// 0b11110xxx -\/ start of 4-\/byte sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1365 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1366             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (char0\_bytes == str\_len) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1367                 \textcolor{comment}{// If we have a 128-\/255 value, we can decode it into a single char:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1368                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (char0\_bytes == 2 \&\& (v0 \& 0xFC) == 0xC0) \{ \textcolor{comment}{// 0x110000xx 0x10xxxxxx}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1369                     one\_char = \textcolor{keyword}{static\_cast<}CharT\textcolor{keyword}{>}(((v0 \& 3) << 6) + (\textcolor{keyword}{static\_cast<}\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}\textcolor{keyword}{>}(\mbox{\hyperlink{classtype__caster__generic_a077b8d1e4af829443b2e41c3e5786f4d}{value}}[1]) \& 0x3F));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1370                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} one\_char;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1371                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1372                 \textcolor{comment}{// Otherwise we have a single character, but it's > U+00FF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1373                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{throw} value\_error(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Character code point not in range(0x100)"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{1374             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1375         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1376 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1377         \textcolor{comment}{// UTF-\/16 is much easier: we can only have a surrogate pair for values above U+FFFF, thus a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1378         \textcolor{comment}{// surrogate pair with total length 2 instantly indicates a range error (but not a "{}your}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1379         \textcolor{comment}{// string was too long"{} error).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1380         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (StringCaster::UTF\_N == 16 \&\& str\_len == 2) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1381             one\_char = \textcolor{keyword}{static\_cast<}CharT\textcolor{keyword}{>}(\mbox{\hyperlink{classtype__caster__generic_a077b8d1e4af829443b2e41c3e5786f4d}{value}}[0]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1382             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (one\_char >= 0xD800 \&\& one\_char < 0xE000)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1383                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{throw} value\_error(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Character code point not in range(0x10000)"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{1384         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1385 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1386         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (str\_len != 1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1387             \textcolor{keywordflow}{throw} value\_error(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Expected a character, but multi-\/character string found"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{1388 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1389         one\_char = \mbox{\hyperlink{classtype__caster__generic_a077b8d1e4af829443b2e41c3e5786f4d}{value}}[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1390         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} one\_char;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1391     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1392 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1393     \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keyword}{constexpr} \textcolor{keyword}{auto} \mbox{\hyperlink{structname}{name}} = \mbox{\hyperlink{descr_8h_a213ce974eda8bd2f9f542dc6e3135355}{\_}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{detail_2common_8h_a4490c1733364f04fcea017da2eb38d38}{PYBIND11\_STRING\_NAME}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{1394     \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} \_T> \textcolor{keyword}{using} \mbox{\hyperlink{structtype__caster_3_01_char_t_00_01enable__if__t_3_01is__std__char__type_3_01_char_t_01_4_1_1value_01_4_01_4_a319a8c4e37e2511027792bed0fc54637}{cast\_op\_type}} = pybind11::detail::cast\_op\_type<\_T>;}

\DoxyCodeLine{1626 \textcolor{comment}{// Our conditions for enabling moving are quite restrictive:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1627 \textcolor{comment}{// At compile time:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1628 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ T needs to be a non-\/const, non-\/pointer, non-\/reference type}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1629 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ type\_caster<T>::operator T\&() must exist}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1630 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ the type must be move constructible (obviously)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1631 \textcolor{comment}{// At run-\/time:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1632 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ if the type is non-\/copy-\/constructible, the object must be the sole owner of the type (i.e. it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1633 \textcolor{comment}{//   must have ref\_count() == 1)h}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1634 \textcolor{comment}{// If any of the above are not satisfied, we fall back to copying.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1635 \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T> \textcolor{keyword}{using} \mbox{\hyperlink{structnegation}{move\_is\_plain\_type}} = \mbox{\hyperlink{structnegation}{satisfies\_none\_of}}<T,}
\DoxyCodeLine{1636     std::is\_void, std::is\_pointer, std::is\_reference, std::is\_const}
\DoxyCodeLine{1637 >;}
